- `12:06` **Jony Yadgar:** Mayor Eric Adams displayed fervency in his speech due to a blend of factors. The unprovoked attack by Hamas on Israel hit close to home considering New York City's significant Jewish population, which is the largest outside of Israel【5†source】【12†source】. This bond between New York City and Israel was emphasized further by Mayor Adams' recent visit to Israel, where he witnessed peaceful coexistence among different faith groups, which Hamas' actions threatened to undermine【12†source】. The attack's timing, coming at the end of Jewish High Holy Days, a celebratory period, likely added to the Mayor's impassioned response, as he saw it as a cowardly act aimed at disturbing the peace and creating division【12†source】.<br><br>In his speech, Mayor Adams drew a comparison between the harmonious living he witnessed in Israel among individuals of Jewish, Muslim, and Christian faiths, and the divisive, violent acts perpetrated by Hamas【12†source】.<br><br>The speech reflects a strong stance against terrorism and a call for solidarity and peace, not only between New York City and Israel but on a broader scale. Mayor Adams' emphasis on ensuring the safety and security of Jewish communities in New York City also highlights the importance of fostering a peaceful and inclusive environment amidst global tensions. His proactive approach in addressing potential threats by coordinating with law enforcement officials and rallying support for Israel showcases a commitment to protecting and standing by allied communities, both locally and internationally【12†source】.
- `12:07` **Jony Yadgar:** Mayor Eric Adams was passionate in his speech because of the close ties between New York City and Israel, particularly due to the large Jewish population in NYC. The Hamas attack on Israel, especially during a significant Jewish holiday period, likely fueled his fervor【5†source】【12†source】.<br><br>He compared the peaceful coexistence he saw among different faith groups in Israel to the violence and division caused by Hamas' actions【12†source】.<br><br>The speech shows his strong stance against terrorism and his commitment to ensuring the safety of Jewish communities both in NYC and in Israel【12†source】.
